# The Russians Aren't Watching (fired by focus)
country_event = {
	id = mongolia.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.1"}
	title = mongolia.1.t
	desc = mongolia.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = RUS
						is_owned_by = TRM
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = MON_russia_claim_state_flag
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mongolia.1.a #Stake our claims on the recognised Mongol lands!

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_PAN_MONGOL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_QING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_JAPAN
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_ISOLATION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_WARPATH
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_SOLO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_QING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_JAPAN
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_state_core = 616 #Ningxia
		remove_ideas = MON_rus_help_less
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mongolia.110 days = 3 }	
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = MON_sternberg

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = XSM modifier = mon_claim_ancient_lands } # -10
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = RUS modifier = mon_claim_ancient_lands } # -10
	}

	option = {
		name = mongolia.1.b #The Chinese be Damned! Unification for ALL the Mongolians!

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_PAN_MONGOL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_QING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_JAPAN
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = MON_path
					option = MON_UNGERN_ISOLATION
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_WARPATH
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_SOLO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_QING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_JAPAN
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_state_core = 616 #Ningxia
		add_state_core = 617 #Urumqi
		add_state_core = 618 #Dzungaria
		remove_ideas = MON_rus_help_less
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mongolia.110 days = 3 }
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = MON_sternberg

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = XSM modifier = mon_unification_XSM } # -10
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = RUS modifier = mon_unification_RUS } # -10
	}

	option = {
		name = mongolia.1.c #It's not worth the risk

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_PAN_MONGOL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_QING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_JAPAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_WARPATH
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_SOLO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_QING
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = MON_path
						option = MON_UNGERN_KHAN_JAPAN
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = MON_path
					option = MON_UNGERN_ISOLATION
				}		
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = mon_no_expansion
	}
}

country_event = { # A Mongol Envoy Arrives
	id = mongolia.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.3"}
	title = mongolia.3.t
	desc = mongolia.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mongolia.3.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }

		MON = { country_event = { id = mongolia.4 days = 4 } }

		hidden_effect = {
		load_oob = "TIB_CAV"
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = MON modifier = TIB_accept_alliance_MON } # 150
	}

	option = {
		name = mongolia.3.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = MON modifier = TIB_refuse_alliance_MON } # -50
	}
}

country_event = { # Tibet accepts our Offer
	id = mongolia.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.4"}
	title = mongolia.4.t
	desc = mongolia.4.d

		name = mongolia.4.a

		create_faction = "Pan-Buddhist National Liberation Front"

		add_to_faction = TIB
		TIB = {
			set_country_flag = allies_with_mongolia
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Ethnic Skirmishes on the Frontier
	id = mongolia.6
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.6"}
	title = mongolia.6.t
	desc = mongolia.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = mongolia.6.a #We shall not stand for this lack of respect! To arms!
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = MON
			type = annex_everything
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = MON modifier = XSM_declares_war_on_Mongolia } # -50
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 283 #Gansu
				SHX = {
					is_subject = no
					has_war = no
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = XSM }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { SHX = { country_event = { id = mongolia.7 days = 1 } } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = mongolia.6.b #Enough blood has been shed. Submit to Sternberg and the Mongols
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_war = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				AND = {
					tag = TAN
					OR = {
						country_exists = SIK
					}
				}
			}
		}
		MON = { puppet = PREV }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 348 #Ningxia
					state = 616 #Inner Mongolia
					state = 617 #Urumqi
					state = 618 #Dzungaria
					state = 621 #Ulanqab
					state = 774 #North Gansu
					AND = {
						state = 1083 # Kumul
						NOT = { is_owned_by = TAN }
					}
				}
			}
			MON = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SIK
				TAN = { is_subject_of = SIK }
			}
			MON = { puppet = TAN }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TIB = { is_in_faction_with = MON }
				owns_state = 353
			}
			TIB = { transfer_state = 353 }
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			MON = { country_event = { id = mongolia.9 days = 1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { TIB = { is_in_faction_with = MON } }
				XSM = { country_event = { id = mongolia.10 days = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Victory in Xibei Lianbang Yiyuan
	id = mongolia.11
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.11"}
	title = mongolia.11.t
	desc = mongolia.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = MON
		owns_state = 618
		NOT = { country_exists = XSM }
	}

	option = {
		name = mongolia.11.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_resource = { type = steel amount = 10 state = 330 }
		add_state_core = 616 #Inner Mongolia
		add_state_core = 617 #Urumqi
		add_state_core = 618 #Dzungaria
		add_state_core = 774 #North Gansu
		add_state_core = 348 #Ningxia
		add_state_core = 1083
		add_state_core = 287
		add_state_core = 619
		add_state_core = 621
		add_state_core = 1085
		add_state_core = 897

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = XSM
				NOT = { is_core_of = MON }
			}
			add_claim_by = MON
		}
		
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SIK
				NOT = { is_core_of = MON }
			}
			add_claim_by = MON
		}
		
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TAN
				NOT = { is_core_of = MON }
			}
			add_claim_by = MON
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = TIB }
			}

			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TIB
					NOT = { is_claimed_by = MON }
					NOT = { is_core_of = MON }
				}
				add_claim_by = MON
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = TIB
			}

			every_state = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = TIB }

				remove_claim_by = MON
			}
		}

		set_global_flag = MON_take_XSM
	}

	option = {
		name = mongolia.11.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }

		add_stability = -0.10

		add_state_core = 616
		add_state_core = 617
		add_state_core = 618

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = XSM NOT = { is_core_of = MON }}

			add_claim_by = MON
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = TIB }
			}

			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = TIB }

				add_claim_by = MON
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = TIB
			}

			every_state = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = TIB }

				remove_claim_by = MON
			}
		}

		set_global_flag = MON_take_XSM
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.1120"}
	title = mongolia.112.t
	desc = mongolia.112.d
	picture = GFX_MON_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = MON
		date > 1942.6.25
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = blue_deal
		}
		MON = { NOT = {has_country_flag = Ja_Lama_control}}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mongolia.112.a
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 78347 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 3423 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
					name = "Genghis Khan II"
					ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
			name = "Amursana"
			desc = ""
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Ja_Lama_II.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = burkhanism_subtype
			traits = {

			}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

				limit = { has_id = 78347 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		random_unit_leader = {

				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		add_stability = 0.05

			name = "Amursana"
			desc = ""
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Ja_Lama_II.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = burkhanism_subtype
			traits = {

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		name = mongolia.113.b

				limit = { has_id = 78347 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}

				limit = { has_id = 3423 }			
				remove_unit_leader = yes
			}
		add_stability = 0.05

			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.02
		}

			popularity = -0.02
		}

			remove_building = {

			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05

	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }

			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
}

		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		name = mongolia.129.b

		}

				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = MON_gonna_free_MON

					name = MON_REL_party

	id = mongolia.158

	picture = GFX_MON_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes

		tag = MON
		date > 1944.5.7
		OR = {
			has_idea = MON_jebtsundamba_khutuktu_NS_idea
			has_idea = MON_jebtsundamba_khutuktu_idea
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mongolia.158.a

			remove_ideas = MON_jebtsundamba_khutuktu_idea

		}

			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Bogd Khan"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {

			limit = {

					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yaroslav I"
				desc = "POLITICS_9TH_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_9th_Jebtsundamba_Khutughtu.png"

				}

		}
	}

country_event = {#
	id = mon_khan.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mon_khan.1" }
	title = mon_khan.1.t
	desc = mon_khan.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_MON_empire_reborn

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#
		name = mon_khan.1.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Genghis Khan II"
			desc = "POLITICS_KHAN_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Genghis_Khan_II.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = occultism_subtype
			traits = {
				MON_spirit_of_genghis
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.70
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			long_name = MON_empire_loyalists_long
			name = MON_empire_loyalists
		}	
		set_cosmetic_tag = MON_empire
		set_country_flag = Gengis_Khan_II_HoS
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = MON_Roman_von_Ungern_Sternberg_cos_sco }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = MON_Roman_von_Ungern_Sternberg_cos_sco
					add_idea = MON_Roman_von_Ungern_Sternberg_khan_cos_sco
				}
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 1157 }
				set_leader_portrait = GFX_Portrait_MON_Genghis_Khan_II
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 1157 }
				set_leader_name = "Genghis Khan II"
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mon_khan.3
	title = mon_khan.3.t
	desc = mon_khan.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mon_khan.3.a
		add_political_power = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = JAP
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = MON_japan_brotherhood_flag
			JAP = {
				set_faction_name = MON_japan_brotherhood
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = MON
					is_subject = no
				}
				add_ideas = Eurasian_alliance_idea
				MON = {	remove_from_faction = PREV }
				JAP = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				add_ideas = Eurasian_alliance_idea
			}
			add_to_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = MON }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = JAP_asian_economic_sphere_member }
				JAP_recalculate_economic_integration = yes
			}
			else = {
				Faction_mergable_invite = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = JAP
					AND = {
						TRM = { is_subject_of = JAP }
					}
					NOT = { has_global_flag = MON_TRM_keep }
				}
			}
			JAP = { end_puppet = TRM }
			puppet = TRM
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = JAP
					TRM = {
						has_socialist_government = no
					}
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				country_event = { id = mon_khan.28 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#release rebellious FNG
	id = mon_khan.5
	title = mon_khan.5.t
	desc = mon_khan.5.d
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = MON
		any_owned_state = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = FNG
				is_core_of = QIE
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = FNG
					is_core_of = QIE
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { country_exists = FNG }
		has_global_flag = MON_new_proposal
		has_global_flag = MON_fengtian_rebellion
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mon_khan.5.a
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = FNG
						is_claimed_by = QIE
						is_core_of = FNG
						is_core_of = QIE
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_chinese_region = yes
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				FNG = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FNG }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FNG
				autonomy_state = kr_special_autonomous_dependency
			}
			FNG = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = FNG_JAP
				set_global_flag = FNG_projapan
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Tang Shaoyi"
					desc = "POLITICS_YANG_YUTING_ARMY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/FNG/Portrait_FNG_Tang_Shaoyi.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = pan_asianism_subtype
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					popularity = 0.4
				}
				clr_country_flag = FNG_communications_clique_active
				clr_country_flag = FNG_recovery_league_active
				clr_country_flag = FNG_zhang_clique_active
				FNG_recalculate_mantetsu_effects = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

			limit = {
				tag = TRK
				has_global_flag = TRK_ilkhanate
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							state = 584
							state = 267
							state = 415
							state = 442
							state = 445
							state = 444
							state = 410
							state = 416
							state = 804
							state = 418
							state = 226
							state = 420
							state = 411
							state = 414
							state = 412
							state = 413
							state = 421
							state = 419
							state = 417
							state = 812
							state = 291
							state = 819
							state = 676
							state = 350
							state = 352
						}
					}
				}
				MON = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			else = {
				MON = {
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = mon_khan.13.b #Accept puppeting(player only)
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		MON = { puppet = PREV }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = mon_khan.13.c #hand over claims(player only)
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core_of = PREV }
				is_core_of = MON
				is_claimed_by = MON
			}
			MON = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = mon_khan_conference.3
	title = mon_khan_conference.3.t
	desc = mon_khan_conference.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = mon_khan_conference.3.a
		set_global_flag = MON_japan_brotherhood_flag
		add_to_array = { global.asian_economic_sphere = MON }
		hidden_effect = {
			MON = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = JAP_asian_economic_sphere_member } }
			JAP_recalculate_economic_integration = yes
		}
		JAP = {
			set_faction_name = MON_japan_brotherhood
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = MON
				is_subject = no
			}
			add_ideas = Eurasian_alliance_idea
			MON = {	remove_from_faction = PREV }
			JAP = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
			add_ideas = Eurasian_alliance_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MON_yiguandao_proposal
			}
			JAP = { add_to_faction = SQI }
			608 = {
				owner = {
					SQI = {
						create_wargoal = {
							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MON_yuan_proposal
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claims_china = yes
						NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_claimed_by = PREV } }
						add_claim_by = PREV
					}
					set_variable = { ambition_area_@PREV = 1 }
				}
			}
			608 = {
				owner = {
					MON = {
						create_wargoal = {
							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MON_qing_proposal
			}
			608 = {
				owner = {
					MON = {
						create_wargoal = {
							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		MON = {
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # event for Transamaur
	id = mon.80
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mon.80" }
	title = mon.80.t
	desc = mon.80.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_refugees
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # we accept them
		name = mon.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TRM }
			MON = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_trait = MON_rvk_member_trait }
					set_nationality = TRM
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			MON = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_trait = MON_rvk_member_trait }
					set_nationality = RUS
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # we don't need them
		name = mon.80.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					tag = TRM 
					RUS = { 
					NOT = { has_government = social_democrat }
					has_socialist_government = no 	
					}
				}
				RUS = { country_event = mon.80 }
			}
			else = {
				MON = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = { has_trait = MON_rvk_member_trait }
					retire = yes
				}
			    }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # russia policy
	id = mon.169
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mon.169" }
	title = mon.169.t
	desc = mon.169.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_DEN_rigspolitiet
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # buddy up with Russia
		name = mon.169.a
		trigger = {
			RUS = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_russia_restored }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MON_russia_friends_flag
		add_political_power = 100
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					RUS = {
						OR = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
							has_left_democratic_government = yes
						}
						NOT = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # we'll go our own way
		name = mon.169.b
		set_country_flag = MON_our_own_way_flag
		set_temp_variable = { target = RUS }
		clear_all_relations_with_TARGET = yes
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -50
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				RUS = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Purge done
	id = mon.177
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mon.177" }
	picture = GFX_report_event_FIN_purges
	title = mon.177.t
	desc = {
		text = mon.177.d_small
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
				value < 2
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = mon.177.d_medium
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
					value = 2
				}
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
					value = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = mon.177.d_big
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
				value > 3
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # cool
		name = mon.177.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
					value < 2
				}
			}
			add_war_support = -0.1
			add_political_power = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
						value = 2
					}
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
						value = 3
					}
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = MON_sternberg_purge_medium_idea
				days = 150
			}
			add_political_power = 150
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = MON_sternberg_purged_someone
					value > 3
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = MON_sternberg_purge_big_idea
				days = 250
			}
			add_political_power = 200
		}
	}
}

	tag = MON
	MON = {
	has_country_leader = { name = "Demchugdongrub" ruling_only = yes }
	is_in_faction_with = JAP
		}
	}

	option = {#
		name = mon.4450.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_political_power = 30
		add_stability = 0.03
	}
	option = {#
		name = mon.4450.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
		JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = MON modifier = medium_increase } }
		set_cosmetic_tag = MON_JAP
	}
	option = {#
		name = mon.4450.c
		ai_chance = { 
		factor = 60 
		modifier = {
				factor = 100
				JAP = { is_ai = no }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -60
		add_stability = -0.06
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 2 }
		add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 2 }
		JAP = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = MON modifier = large_increase } }
		if = {
		limit = {
		MON = { is_ai = yes }
		}
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = MON
				autonomy_state = kr_nominal_puppet
				end_wars = no
			}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = MON_JAP_MEN
	}

country_event = { # Mongolia Chinese Puppet Unfuck
	id = mon.750
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mon.750" }
	title = mon.750.t
	desc = mon.750.d

	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = MON
		has_autonomy_state = kr_governorate
		is_subject = yes
		overlord = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
		OR = {
		has_country_leader = { name = "Roman von Ungern-Sternberg" ruling_only = yes }
		has_country_leader = { name = "Genghis Khan II" ruling_only = yes }
		}
	}
    fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = mon.750.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Jodbajab"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Jodbajab.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = pataut_warlordism_subtype
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			long_name = XSM_syndicalist_party_long
			name = XSM_syndicalist_party
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = mongolia_non_sternberg keep_completed = no }
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1157 }			
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { overlord = { tag = CHI } }
			set_cosmetic_tag = MON_KMT
		}
		else = { set_cosmetic_tag = MON_BASIC_PUPPET }
	}
}

country_event = { #Work with MAN or Nah
	id = tot_mon.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.10"}
	title = tot_mon.7.t
	desc = tot_mon.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MON_red_empire
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Work With Em
		name = tot_mon.7.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = radical_socialist } }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = radical_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_tot_pop = party_popularity@totalist
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_radsoc_pop = party_popularity@radical_socialist
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_tot_pop
				value = current_radsoc_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = current_tot_pop
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Gada Meiren"
				desc = "POLITICS_GADA_MEIREN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Gada_Meiren.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = radsoc_indigenous_communitarianism_subtype
				traits = {}
			}  
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = radical_socialist }
			set_country_leader_ideology = radsoc_indigenous_communitarianism_subtype
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_tot_to_coalition = yes
	}
	option = { #Nah
		name = tot_mon.7.b

			limit = { NOT = { has_government = totalist } }

				ruling_party = totalist

			set_variable = {

			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_radsoc_pop
				value = current_tot_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = current_radsoc_pop
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Gada Meiren"
				desc = "POLITICS_GADA_MEIREN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Gada_Meiren.png"

		}

		}

			set_party_name = {

country_event = { #Roerich Mongolia
	id = tot_mon_flavor.37
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.37"}
	title = tot_mon_flavor.37.t
	desc = tot_mon_flavor.37.d
	picture = GFX_news_roerich_sikkim
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.37.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 80 }
		add_stability = 0.01
	}
	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.37.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = totalist } }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_radsoc_pop = party_popularity@radical_socialist
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_tot_pop = party_popularity@totalist
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_radsoc_pop
				value = current_tot_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalist
				popularity = current_radsoc_pop
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Gada Meiren"
				desc = "POLITICS_GADA_MEIREN_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/MON/Portrait_MON_Gada_Meiren.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = esoteric_leninism_subtype
				traits = {}
			}  
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = totalist }
			set_country_leader_ideology = esoteric_leninism_subtype
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = MON_ROERICH
		add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
	}
}

	id = tot_mon_flavor.31
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event mongolia.10"}
	title = tot_mon_flavor.31.t
	desc = tot_mon_flavor.31.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.31.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 } # for balance (or do you want Internationale fighting all the world because of Mongolia claims?)
		trigger = { FRA = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
		FRA = { add_to_faction = MON }
	}
	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.31.b
		ai_chance = { base = 10 } # for balance
		trigger = { BHC = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
		BHC = { add_to_faction = MON }
	}
	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.31.c
		ai_chance = { base = 65 } # for balance (or do you want Internationale fighting all the world because of Mongolia claims?)
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Dorjjavyn Luvsansharav"
						ruling_only = yes
					} 
				}
				create_faction = "Comintern"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Ulanhu"
						ruling_only = yes
					} 
				}
				create_faction = "United Revolutionary Front"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Gada Meiren"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				create_faction = "The Red Horde"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = radical_socialist
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Gada Meiren"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				create_faction = "Universal Social Kinship of All Under the Sky"
			}
		}
	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.31.e
		ai_chance = { base = 20 } # for balance (or do you want Internationale fighting all the world because of Mongolia claims?)
		trigger = {
			SKM = {
				has_socialist_government = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
		}
		SKM = { add_to_faction = MON }
	}
	option = { #Wholesome
		name = tot_mon_flavor.31.f
		ai_chance = { base = 5 } # for balance (or do you want Internationale fighting all the world because of Mongolia claims?)
		add_ideas = MON_isolation_in_steppe
	}
}
